<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aflossen.html>aflossen</a> (14764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:aflossen.html>aflossen</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lossen.html>lossen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
